<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непременный.html>непреме́нный</a> (12085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">непрѣмѣньнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neprěměnĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare inherited <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переменный.html>переме́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereménnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">variable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемена.html>переме́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereména</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">change</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">преста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prestátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непрестанный.html>непреста́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprestánnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)непреста́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)непреста́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ceaseless, unceasing, incessant</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непривычка.html>непривы́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprivýčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непривычка.html>непривы́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непривычка.html>непривы́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непривычка.html>непривы́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lack of habit

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:непривычка.html>непривы́чки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́лось</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудный.html>тру́дным</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>neprivýčki</b> éto kazálosʹ trúdnym</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it seemed difficult because one was not used to it</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***неприглядный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприглядный.html>непригля́дный</a> (19974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пригляд(е́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prigljad(étʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприглядный.html>непригля́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprigljádnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unsightly, unattractive</li></ol>

***неприкаянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприкаянный.html>неприка́янный</a> (21286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Has the form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*прика́янный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*prikájannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, putative past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*прика́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*prikájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каяться.html>ка́яться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kájatʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to repent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаянный.html>окая́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okajánnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">damned, cursed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкаянный.html>неприка́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprikájannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неприка́яннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неприка́янней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> restless, not knowing what to do</li>
<li>unsettled, homeless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенность.html>неприкоснове́нность</a> (18212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neprikosnovénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>inviolability
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенность.html>неприкоснове́нность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:личность.html>ли́чности</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprikosnovénnostʹ</b> líčnosti</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">personal immunity</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенность.html>неприкоснове́нность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилище.html>жили́ща</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprikosnovénnostʹ</b> žilíšča</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">inviolability/sanctity of the home</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенность.html>неприкоснове́нность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чной</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:частный.html>ча́стной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprikosnovénnostʹ</b> ličnoj/částnoj žízni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">privacy</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a> (21711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprikosnovénnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>untouchable, inviolable, immune, sacrosanct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reserve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprikosnovénnyj</b> zapás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reserve supply</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The term is not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неприкаса́емый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neprikasájemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мый</a> (11411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprimirímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>irreconcilable, unappeasable, implacable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprimirímaja</b> borʹbá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">uncompromising struggle; war to the knife</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьбу́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vesti <b>neprimirímuju</b> borʹbú (prótiv)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wage a relentless struggle (against)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>incompatible, irreconcilable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprimirímyje</b> protivoréčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">irreconcilable contradictions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непринужденный.html>непринуждённый</a> (10584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принуждённый.html>принуждённый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinuždjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непринужденный.html>непринуждённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprinuždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unconstrained</li>
<li>informal</li>
<li>unforced, unstrained</li>
<li>at ease <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">free of anxiety</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>easy, free, natural, casual (speech, manners, etc.)</li>
<li>spontaneous, unstudied</li>
<li>unrestrained</li>
<li>unaffected</li>
<li>cavalier</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприступный.html>непристу́пный</a> (11133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приступ.html>при́ступ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prístup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприступный.html>непристу́пный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nepristúpnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inaccessible, unapproachable, forbidding</li>

***неприятность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тность</a> (2696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятный.html>неприя́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neprijátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprijátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slovenliness, unpleasantness</li>
<li>trouble</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непроглядный.html>непрогля́дный</a> (14540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">прогляд(е́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">progljad(étʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непроглядный.html>непрогля́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprogljádnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)непрогля́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)непрогля́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pitch-black</li>
<li>impenetrable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроглядный.html>непрогля́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprogljádnaja</b> nočʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pitch-black night</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроглядный.html>непрогля́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprogljádnyj</b> tumán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">impenetrable fog</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
